// FUNGSI SYNC DENGAN CHUNKING SYSTEM (TAMBAHKAN BARU)
function syncDataMuridWithNotesEnhancedAmanChunked(maxRows = 20) {
  try {
    const resumeKey = `${RESUME_PROPERTIES.SYNC_DATA}_Data_Murid`;
    let resumeState = getResumeState(resumeKey);
    let startTime = new Date().getTime();
    
    if (!resumeState) {
      console.log('🔄 Memulai sync chunked data murid...');
      
      // 1. Ambil data dari API
      const url = `${API_BASE_URL}?action=get_murid`;
      const options = { 
        'muteHttpExceptions': true, 
        'timeout': 30000 
      };
      
      const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
      const result = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
      
      if (!result.success) {
        throw new Error(result.error || 'API error');
      }
      
      const data = result.data || [];
      console.log(`📊 ${data.length} data murid ditemukan`);
      
      if (data.length === 0) {
        return 'Tidak ada data murid';
      }
      
      // 2. Buat atau clear sheet
      const spreadsheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
      let sheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName('Data_Murid');
      
      if (!sheet) {
        sheet = spreadsheet.insertSheet('Data_Murid');
      } else {
        // Clear hanya data, bukan header
        if (sheet.getLastRow() > 1) {
          sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).clearContent();
        }
      }
      
      // 3. Set header
      const headers = [
        'murid_id', 'nama', 'nis', 'nik', 
        'no_hp', 'alamat', 'nama_wali', 'no_wali', 
        'nilai', 'foto', 'kelas_madin_id', 'kelas_quran_id', 
        'kamar_id', 'created_at', 'updated_at'
      ];
      
      sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length)
        .setValues([headers])
        .setFontWeight('bold')
        .setBackground('#4CAF50')
        .setFontColor('white');
      
      // 4. Simpan data ke Properties untuk diproses chunk
      const syncData = {
        allData: data,
        headers: headers,
        currentIndex: 0,
        totalRows: data.length,
        startTime: startTime
      };
      
      setResumeState(resumeKey, syncData);
      resumeState = syncData;
      
      console.log(`📦 Data disimpan untuk diproses per ${maxRows} baris`);
    }
    
    // 5. Proses chunk
    const data = resumeState.allData;
    const headers = resumeState.headers;
    let currentIndex = resumeState.currentIndex || 0;
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName('Data_Murid');
    
    const chunkEnd = Math.min(currentIndex + maxRows, data.length);
    console.log(`🔄 Processing rows ${currentIndex + 1} to ${chunkEnd} of ${data.length}`);
    
    // Isi data chunk
    const rows = [];
    for (let i = currentIndex; i < chunkEnd; i++) {
      const item = data[i];
      rows.push(headers.map(header => 
        item[header] !== undefined && item[header] !== null ? item[header] : ''
      ));
    }
    
    if (rows.length > 0) {
      const startRow = currentIndex + 2; // +2 karena baris 1 header
      sheet.getRange(startRow, 1, rows.length, headers.length).setValues(rows);
    }
    
    // Update progress
    resumeState.currentIndex = chunkEnd;
    resumeState.lastUpdated = new Date().toISOString();
    
    // Cek jika selesai
    if (chunkEnd >= data.length) {
      console.log(`✅ Sync chunked selesai: ${data.length} data`);
      
      // Tambahkan notes dan formatting
      setTimeout(() => {
        syncReferensiData();
        Utilities.sleep(2000);
        
        const refData = getReferensiData();
        fillNotesInBatchEnhanced(sheet, headers, refData);
        setColumnFormats(sheet, headers);
        
        for (let col = 1; col <= headers.length; col++) {
          sheet.autoResizeColumn(col);
        }
        
        setupSimpleDataValidation(sheet, headers, refData);
      }, 1000);
      
      setResumeState(resumeKey, null);
      
      SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().toast(
        `✅ Sync berhasil: ${data.length} data`,
        'Sync Chunked Complete',
        5
      );
      
      return `SUCCESS: ${data.length} data murid disinkronisasi (chunked)`;
    } else {
      setResumeState(resumeKey, resumeState);
      
      const progress = Math.round((chunkEnd / data.length) * 100);
      const message = `⏸️ Sync dijeda: ${chunkEnd}/${data.length} baris (${progress}%)`;
      
      console.log(message);
      
      SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().toast(
        `Sync progress: ${progress}%. Jalankan lagi untuk melanjutkan.`,
        'Sync in Progress',
        8
      );
      
      return message;
    }
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(`❌ Sync chunked gagal: ${error.toString()}`);
    return `ERROR: ${error.toString()}`;
  }
}

function syncDataMuridOptimal() {
  try {
    console.log('🚀 Memulai sync data murid optimal...');
    
    const spreadsheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    spreadsheet.toast('Sync data murid optimal dimulai...', 'Info', 3);
    
    // 1. SYNC DATA REFERENSI DULU
    console.log('🔄 Syncing data referensi...');
    syncReferensiData();
    Utilities.sleep(3000); // Beri waktu untuk referensi tersimpan
    
    // 2. AMBIL DATA DARI API
    console.log('🔗 Mengambil data murid dari API...');
    const url = `${API_BASE_URL}?action=get_murid`;
    const options = { 
      'muteHttpExceptions': true, 
      'timeout': 30000 
    };
    
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
    const result = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
    
    if (!result.success) {
      throw new Error(result.error || 'API error');
    }
    
    const data = result.data || [];
    console.log(`📊 ${data.length} data murid ditemukan`);
    
    if (data.length === 0) {
      return 'Tidak ada data murid';
    }
    
    // 3. BUAT SHEET SEMENTARA
    const timestamp = new Date().getTime();
    const tempSheetName = `Data_Murid_TEMP_${timestamp}`;
    const tempSheet = spreadsheet.insertSheet(tempSheetName);
    
    // 4. SET HEADER YANG BENAR
    const headers = [
      'murid_id', 'nama', 'nis', 'nik', 
      'no_hp', 'alamat', 'nama_wali', 'no_wali', 
      'nilai', 'foto', 'kelas_madin_id', 'kelas_quran_id', 
      'kamar_id', 'created_at', 'updated_at'
    ];
    
    tempSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length)
      .setValues([headers])
      .setFontWeight('bold')
      .setBackground('#4CAF50')
      .setFontColor('white');
    
    // 5. ISI DATA DENGAN BATCH (UNTUK HINDARI TIMEOUT)
    console.log('📥 Mengisi data ke sheet...');
    
    // Gunakan batch size yang optimal
    const batchSize = 100;
    const totalBatches = Math.ceil(data.length / batchSize);
    
    for (let batch = 0; batch < totalBatches; batch++) {
      const startIdx = batch * batchSize;
      const endIdx = Math.min(startIdx + batchSize, data.length);
      
      console.log(`🔄 Batch ${batch + 1}/${totalBatches}: Baris ${startIdx + 1} sampai ${endIdx}`);
      
      const batchData = data.slice(startIdx, endIdx);
      const rows = batchData.map(item => 
        headers.map(header => item[header] !== undefined && item[header] !== null ? item[header] : '')
      );
      
      const startRow = startIdx + 2; // +2 karena baris 1 header
      tempSheet.getRange(startRow, 1, rows.length, headers.length).setValues(rows);
      
      // Progress update
      const progress = Math.round(((batch + 1) / totalBatches) * 100);
      if (progress % 20 === 0) {
        console.log(`📈 Progress: ${progress}%`);
      }
      
      // Delay kecil antar batch untuk stabilisasi
      if (batch < totalBatches - 1) {
        Utilities.sleep(1000);
      }
    }
    
    // 6. DAPATKAN DATA REFERENSI UNTUK NOTES
    console.log('🗺️ Memuat data referensi untuk notes...');
    const refData = getReferensiData();
    
    console.log('📊 Data referensi loaded:', {
      kelas_madin: Object.keys(refData.kelas_madin_id || {}).length,
      kelas_quran: Object.keys(refData.kelas_quran_id || {}).length,
      kamar: Object.keys(refData.kamar_id || {}).length
    });
    
    // 7. ISI NOTES DENGAN METODE SEDERHANA YANG PASTI BEKERJA
    console.log('📝 Mengisi notes...');
    const notesResult = fillNotesSederhana(tempSheet, headers, refData);
    console.log(`✅ Notes result: ${notesResult.notesAdded} notes added`);
    
    // 8. FORMAT KOLOM
    setColumnFormats(tempSheet, headers);
    
    // 9. GANTI SHEET LAMA
    const oldSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName('Data_Murid');
    if (oldSheet) {
      spreadsheet.deleteSheet(oldSheet);
    }
    
    tempSheet.setName('Data_Murid');
    
    // 10. AUTO RESIZE
    for (let col = 1; col <= headers.length; col++) {
      tempSheet.autoResizeColumn(col);
    }
    
    // 11. SETUP DATA VALIDATION SEDERHANA
    setupSimpleDataValidation(tempSheet, headers, refData);
    
    const successMsg = `SUCCESS: ${data.length} data murid dengan ${notesResult.notesAdded} notes`;
    console.log(`✅ ${successMsg}`);
    
    spreadsheet.toast(
      `✅ Sync berhasil: ${data.length} data murid`,
      'Sync Optimal',
      5
    );
    
    return successMsg;
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(`❌ Sync optimal gagal: ${error.toString()}`);
    return `ERROR: ${error.toString()}`;
  }
}

function syncDataMuridSimple() {
  try {
    console.log('🚀 Sync data murid simple...');
    
    // 1. Ambil data dari API
    const url = `${API_BASE_URL}?action=get_murid`;
    const options = { 'muteHttpExceptions': true, 'timeout': 30000 };
    
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
    const result = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
    
    if (!result.success) {
      throw new Error(result.error || 'API error');
    }
    
    const data = result.data || [];
    console.log(`📊 ${data.length} data murid ditemukan`);
    
    if (data.length === 0) {
      return 'Tidak ada data murid';
    }
    
    // 2. Buat sheet
    const sheet = buatSheet('Data_Murid');
    
    // 3. Set header
    const headers = [
      'murid_id', 'nama', 'nis', 'nik', 
      'no_hp', 'alamat', 'nama_wali', 'no_wali', 
      'nilai', 'foto', 'kelas_madin_id', 'kelas_quran_id', 
      'kamar_id', 'created_at', 'updated_at'
    ];
    
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length)
      .setValues([headers])
      .setFontWeight('bold')
      .setBackground('#4CAF50')
      .setFontColor('white');
    
    // 4. Isi data
    const rows = data.map(item => 
      headers.map(header => item[header] !== undefined && item[header] !== null ? item[header] : '')
    );
    
    if (rows.length > 0) {
      sheet.getRange(2, 1, rows.length, headers.length).setValues(rows);
    }
    
    // 5. Dapatkan data referensi
    const refData = getReferensiData();
    
    // 6. Isi notes dengan metode yang sederhana
    const notesResult = fillNotesSederhana(sheet, headers, refData);
    
    // 7. Format kolom
    setColumnFormats(sheet, headers);
    
    // 8. Auto resize
    for (let col = 1; col <= headers.length; col++) {
      sheet.autoResizeColumn(col);
    }
    
    const successMsg = `SUCCESS: ${data.length} data murid dengan ${notesResult.notesAdded} notes`;
    console.log(`✅ ${successMsg}`);
    
    SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().toast(
      `✅ Sync simple berhasil: ${data.length} data`,
      'Sync Simple',
      5
    );
    
    return successMsg;
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(`❌ Sync simple gagal: ${error.toString()}`);
    return `ERROR: ${error.toString()}`;
  }
}

function jalankanSyncMuridDenganNotes() {
  try {
    const spreadsheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    
    // Tampilkan dialog pilihan
    const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
    const response = ui.alert(
      'Pilih Metode Sync Data Murid',
      'Pilih metode sinkronisasi data murid:\n\n' +
      '1. 🔄 **Sync Optimal** (Direkomendasikan)\n' +
      '   - Untuk data banyak\n' +
      '   - Menggunakan batch processing\n' +
      '   - Lebih stabil\n\n' +
      '2. ⚡ **Sync Simple**\n' +
      '   - Untuk data sedikit (< 100 baris)\n' +
      '   - Lebih cepat\n' +
      '   - Notes langsung terisi\n\n' +
      '3. ⏯️ **Sync dengan Resume**\n' +
      '   - Untuk data sangat banyak\n' +
      '   - Bisa dilanjutkan jika timeout',
      ui.ButtonSet.YES_NO_CANCEL
    );
    
    let result;
    
    if (response === ui.Button.YES) {
      // Sync Optimal
      spreadsheet.toast('Memulai sync optimal...', 'Info', 3);
      result = syncDataMuridOptimal();
    } else if (response === ui.Button.NO) {
      // Sync Simple
      spreadsheet.toast('Memulai sync simple...', 'Info', 3);
      result = syncDataMuridSimple();
    } else {
      // Sync dengan Resume
      spreadsheet.toast('Memulai sync dengan resume...', 'Info', 3);
      result = syncDataMuridWithNotesEnhancedAmanChunked(15);
    }
    
    // Tampilkan hasil
    ui.alert('Hasil Sync Data Murid', result, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    
    return result;
    
  } catch (error) {
    const errorMsg = `❌ Error menjalankan sync: ${error.toString()}`;
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('Error', errorMsg, SpreadsheetApp.getUi().ButtonSet.OK);
    return errorMsg;
  }
}

// Fungsi yang belum ada tapi dipanggil di menu
function syncSemuaDataViaAPI() {
  try {
    console.log('🚀 Memulai sinkronisasi semua data...');
    
    const results = [];
    
    // Sync referensi dulu
    results.push('🔄 Sync Referensi...');
    syncReferensiData();
    Utilities.sleep(3000);
    
    // Sync data utama
    const syncFunctions = [
      { name: 'Murid', func: syncDataMuridSimple },
      { name: 'Guru', func: syncDataGuruViaAPI },
      { name: 'Users', func: syncDataUsersViaAPI },
      { name: 'Alumni', func: syncDataAlumniViaAPI }
    ];
    
    for (const task of syncFunctions) {
      try {
        results.push(`🔄 ${task.name}...`);
        const result = task.func();
        results.push(`✅ ${task.name}: ${result.includes('SUCCESS') ? 'Berhasil' : 'Periksa log'}`);
        Utilities.sleep(2000);
      } catch (error) {
        results.push(`❌ ${task.name}: Error`);
      }
    }
    
    // Setup trigger jika belum ada
    if (!checkEditTrigger()) {
      setupSimpleEditTrigger();
      results.push('✅ Trigger Auto Sync diaktifkan');
    }
    
    // Tampilkan hasil
    const message = `📊 HASIL SYNCRONISASI:\n\n${results.join('\n')}`;
    
    const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
    ui.alert('✅ Sync Selesai', message, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    
    return results;
    
  } catch (error) {
    const errorMsg = `❌ Sync gagal: ${error.toString()}`;
    console.error(errorMsg);
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('❌ Error', errorMsg, SpreadsheetApp.getUi().ButtonSet.OK);
    return [errorMsg];
  }
}

// =============================================
// 7. FUNGSI PUSH DATA (SHEET → API)
// =============================================
function updateDataToMySQL(table, data, where) {
  try {
    if (!table || typeof table !== 'string' || table.trim() === '') {
      throw new Error('Nama tabel tidak valid atau kosong');
    }
    
    if (!data || typeof data !== 'object' || Object.keys(data).length === 0) {
      throw new Error('Data tidak valid atau kosong');
    }
    
    if (!where || typeof where !== 'object' || Object.keys(where).length === 0) {
      throw new Error('Kondisi where tidak valid atau kosong');
    }

    const cleanData = {};
    Object.keys(data).forEach(key => {
      const value = data[key];
      
      if (value === undefined || value === null) {
        return;
      }
      
      if (typeof value === 'string' && value.trim() === '') {
        cleanData[key] = null;
      } else {
        cleanData[key] = value;
      }
    });
    
    if (Object.keys(cleanData).length === 0) {
      throw new Error('Tidak ada data yang valid untuk diupdate');
    }
    
    const payload = {
      table: table,
      action: 'update',
      data: cleanData,
      where: where
    };
    
    Logger.log(`📤 Update ke ${table}: ${JSON.stringify(payload).substring(0, 200)}...`);
    
    const options = {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      payload: JSON.stringify(payload),
      'muteHttpExceptions': true,
      'timeout': 30000,
      'followRedirects': true
    };
    
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(API_UPDATE_URL, options);
    const responseCode = response.getResponseCode();
    const responseText = response.getContentText();
    
    Logger.log(`📊 Response Code: ${responseCode}`);
    
    if (responseCode !== 200) {
      throw new Error(`HTTP ${responseCode}: ${responseText.substring(0, 200)}`);
    }
    
    if (responseText.trim() === '' || 
        responseText.includes('<!DOCTYPE') || 
        responseText.includes('<html')) {
      throw new Error('Server returned non-JSON response');
    }
    
    const result = JSON.parse(responseText);
    
    if (result.success) {
      Logger.log(`✅ Berhasil update ${table}: ${result.affected_rows || 1} baris`);
      return result;
    } else {
      const errorMsg = result.error || 'Unknown error from API';
      
      if (errorMsg.includes('Duplicate entry')) {
        Logger.log(`⚠️ Duplicate entry: ${errorMsg}`);
        return { success: false, error: errorMsg, duplicate: true };
      } else if (errorMsg.includes('Data too long')) {
        Logger.log(`⚠️ Data too long: ${errorMsg}`);
        return { success: false, error: errorMsg, dataTooLong: true };
      } else if (errorMsg.includes('doesn\'t exist')) {
        Logger.log(`⚠️ Column doesn't exist: ${errorMsg}`);
        return { success: false, error: errorMsg, invalidColumn: true };
      } else {
        throw new Error(errorMsg);
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {
    Logger.log(`❌ Gagal update ke ${table}: ${error.toString()}`);
    throw error;
  }
}

function prepareDataDirect(headers, rowData, sheetName) {
  try {
    console.log(`🔧 Preparing direct data for ${sheetName}...`);
    
    const data = {};
    const whereCondition = {};
    
    for (let i = 0; i < headers.length; i++) {
      const header = headers[i];
      const value = rowData[i];
      
      if (!header || value === undefined || value === null || value === '') {
        continue;
      }
      
      const cleanHeader = header.toString().toLowerCase().trim();
      
      if (cleanHeader.includes('_id')) {
        whereCondition[header] = value;
      }
      
      data[header] = value;
    }
    
    if (Object.keys(whereCondition).length === 0) {
      const idField = getPrimaryKeyForTable(sheetName);
      const idIndex = headers.findIndex(h => 
        h.toString().toLowerCase().includes(idField)
      );
      
      if (idIndex !== -1 && rowData[idIndex]) {
        whereCondition[headers[idIndex]] = rowData[idIndex];
      }
    }
    
    console.log(`📤 Prepared data for ${sheetName}:`, { data, whereCondition });
    
    return {
      table: sheetName,
      action: 'update',
      data: data,
      where: whereCondition
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(`❌ Error prepareDataDirect: ${error.toString()}`);
    return null;
  }
}

function pushSheetDataOptimized(sheetName) {
  try {
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(sheetName);
    if (!sheet) {
      return { success: false, error: 'Sheet tidak ditemukan', successCount: 0, errorCount: 1, skippedCount: 0 };
    }
    
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0];
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      return { success: true, message: 'Tidak ada data', successCount: 0, errorCount: 0, skippedCount: 0 };
    }
    
    // Cek state resume
    const resumeKey = `${RESUME_PROPERTIES.PUSH_DATA}_${sheetName}`;
    let resumeState = getResumeState(resumeKey);
    let startRow = 1;
    let successCount = 0, errorCount = 0, skippedCount = 0;
    
    if (resumeState) {
      console.log(`🔄 RESUMING ${sheetName} dari baris ${resumeState.lastProcessedRow}`);
      startRow = resumeState.lastProcessedRow;
      successCount = resumeState.successCount || 0;
      errorCount = resumeState.errorCount || 0;
      skippedCount = resumeState.skippedCount || 0;
    } else {
      console.log(`🔄 STARTING NEW ${sheetName}: ${data.length-1} rows`);
      resumeState = initializeResumeProgress(sheetName, data.length - 1);
    }
    
    // Adaptive chunk size berdasarkan pengalaman
    const chunkSize = Math.min(5, Math.max(2, Math.ceil((data.length - startRow) / 10)));
    const maxChunks = 3; // Maksimal 3 chunk per eksekusi
    
    console.log(`⚡ Processing ${chunkSize} rows per chunk, max ${maxChunks} chunks`);
    
    for (let chunk = 0; chunk < maxChunks; chunk++) {
      const currentRow = startRow + (chunk * chunkSize);
      const endRow = Math.min(currentRow + chunkSize, data.length);
      
      if (currentRow >= data.length) break;
      
      console.log(`📦 Chunk ${chunk+1}: Rows ${currentRow} to ${endRow-1}`);
      
      for (let i = currentRow; i < endRow; i++) {
        const rowData = data[i];
        
        if (isRowEmpty(rowData)) {
          skippedCount++;
          continue;
        }
        
        const preparation = prepareDataDirect(headers, rowData, sheetName);
        
        if (!preparation.isValid) {
          skippedCount++;
          continue;
        }
        
        try {
          const result = updateDataToMySQL(
            getTableName(sheetName), 
            preparation.updateData, 
            preparation.whereCondition
          );
          
          if (result && result.success) {
            successCount++;
          } else if (result && result.skipped) {
            skippedCount++;
          } else {
            errorCount++;
          }
        } catch (error) {
          errorCount++;
          console.log(`❌ Row ${i+1} error: ${error.toString().substring(0, 100)}`);
        }
        
        // Update resume state setiap baris
        resumeState.lastProcessedRow = i + 1;
        resumeState.successCount = successCount;
        resumeState.errorCount = errorCount;
        resumeState.skippedCount = skippedCount;
        resumeState.lastUpdated = new Date().toISOString();
        
        setResumeState(resumeKey, resumeState);
      }
      
      // Delay antar chunk untuk menghindari rate limit
      if (chunk < maxChunks - 1 && (endRow < data.length)) {
        Utilities.sleep(2000);
      }
    }
    
    // Cek jika sudah selesai
    if (resumeState.lastProcessedRow >= data.length) {
      console.log(`✅ ${sheetName} COMPLETED: ${successCount}✅ ${errorCount}❌ ${skippedCount}⏩`);
      setResumeState(resumeKey, null); // Clear resume state
      
      return {
        success: errorCount === 0,
        successCount, errorCount, skippedCount,
        totalProcessed: successCount + errorCount + skippedCount,
        completed: true
      };
    } else {
      console.log(`⏸️ ${sheetName} PAUSED: ${successCount}✅ ${errorCount}❌ ${skippedCount}⏩`);
      console.log(`📌 Progress: ${resumeState.lastProcessedRow-1}/${data.length-1} rows`);
      
      // Tampilkan notifikasi untuk melanjutkan
      SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().toast(
        `Push data ${sheetName} dijeda di baris ${resumeState.lastProcessedRow}. Jalankan lagi untuk melanjutkan.`,
        '⏸️ Push Dijeda',
        10
      );
      
      return {
        success: false,
        successCount, errorCount, skippedCount,
        completed: false,
        resumeAt: resumeState.lastProcessedRow,
        totalRows: data.length - 1,
        message: `PAUSED at row ${resumeState.lastProcessedRow}. Run again to continue.`
      };
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(`❌ Optimized processing failed: ${error.toString()}`);
    return {
      success: false,
      error: error.toString(),
      successCount: 0, errorCount: 1, skippedCount: 0
    };
  }
}

function pushAllDataChunked() {
  console.log('🚀 Memulai push data chunked...');
  
  const sheetsToPush = ['Data_Guru', 'Data_Murid', 'Data_Users', 'Data_Alumni'];
  const results = [];
  
  sheetsToPush.forEach(sheetName => {
    try {
      console.log(`📤 Processing ${sheetName}...`);
      const result = pushSheetDataOptimized(sheetName);
      results.push({
        sheet: sheetName,
        ...result
      });
      
      if (!result.completed) {
        console.log(`⏸️ ${sheetName} perlu dilanjutkan`);
        // Hentikan loop jika ada yang belum selesai
        throw new Error(`PAUSED at ${sheetName}`);
      }
      
      Utilities.sleep(3000); // Delay antar sheet
    } catch (error) {
      if (error.message.includes('PAUSED')) {
        results.push({
          sheet: sheetName,
          paused: true,
          message: error.message
        });
      } else {
        results.push({
          sheet: sheetName,
          error: error.toString()
        });
      }
    }
  });
  
  // Tampilkan summary
  const completed = results.filter(r => r.completed || r.success).length;
  const total = sheetsToPush.length;
  
  const summary = `📊 PUSH CHUNKED RESULTS:\n` +
    `✅ ${completed}/${total} sheets completed\n` +
    `⏸️ ${results.filter(r => r.paused).length} paused\n` +
    results.map(r => 
      `• ${r.sheet}: ${r.completed ? '✅' : r.paused ? '⏸️' : '❌'} ${r.message || ''}`
    ).join('\n');
  
  console.log(summary);
  
  const sheet = buatSummarySheet();
  sheet.clear();
  sheet.getRange(1, 1).setValue(summary);
  sheet.autoResizeColumn(1);
  
  return results;
}

function prepareDataForUpdateValidated(headers, rowData, sheetName) {
  const updateData = {};
  const whereCondition = {};
  let primaryKeyFound = false;

  try {
    // Dapatkan struktur tabel dari database
    const tableName = getTableName(sheetName);
    const dbStructure = getDatabaseTableStructure(tableName);
    
    if (!dbStructure) {
      Logger.log(`⚠️ Tidak bisa mendapatkan struktur untuk ${tableName}, gunakan fallback`);
      return prepareDataForUpdateUniversal(headers, rowData, sheetName);
    }

    const dbColumns = dbStructure.map(col => col.Field || col.column_name);
    Logger.log(`✅ Kolom valid di ${tableName}: ${dbColumns.join(', ')}`);

    headers.forEach((header, index) => {
      if (!header || header.toString().trim() === '') return;

      const headerName = header.toString().trim();
      let value = rowData[index];

      // Handle empty values
      if (value === '' || value === undefined || value === null) {
        value = null;
      }

      // Hanya proses kolom yang ada di database
      if (!dbColumns.includes(headerName)) {
        Logger.log(`⏩ Skip kolom ${headerName} - tidak ada di database`);
        return;
      }

      const cleanHeader = headerName.toLowerCase();

      // Identifikasi primary key
      if ((cleanHeader === 'id' || cleanHeader.includes('_id')) && value) {
        whereCondition[headerName] = value;
        primaryKeyFound = true;
      } 
      // Field data untuk update
      else if (!['created_at', 'updated_at', 'timestamp'].includes(cleanHeader)) {
        updateData[headerName] = value;
      }
    });

    // Fallback jika tidak ada primary key
    if (!primaryKeyFound) {
      const uniqueFields = ['email', 'nis', 'nik', 'nama', 'no_hp'];
      for (let i = 0; i < headers.length; i++) {
        const header = headers[i].toString().trim();
        const cleanHeader = header.toLowerCase();
        if (uniqueFields.includes(cleanHeader) && rowData[i] && dbColumns.includes(header)) {
          whereCondition[header] = rowData[i];
          primaryKeyFound = true;
          break;
        }
      }
    }

    Logger.log(`🔧 Validated data for ${sheetName}:`);
    Logger.log(`   Where: ${JSON.stringify(whereCondition)}`);
    Logger.log(`   Update: ${JSON.stringify(updateData)}`);

    return {
      updateData: updateData,
      whereCondition: whereCondition,
      isValid: primaryKeyFound && Object.keys(updateData).length > 0,
      error: !primaryKeyFound ? 'Tidak ditemukan primary key yang valid' : 
             Object.keys(updateData).length === 0 ? 'Tidak ada data yang akan diupdate' : null
    };

  } catch (error) {
    Logger.log(`❌ Error validated preparation: ${error}`);
    // Fallback ke universal approach
    return prepareDataForUpdateUniversal(headers, rowData, sheetName);
  }
}

function prepareDataForUpdateUniversal(headers, rowData, sheetName) {
  const updateData = {};
  const whereCondition = {};
  let primaryKeyFound = false;

  const invalidColumnsForMurid = ['kelas_madin', 'kelas_quran', 'kamar'];
  
  headers.forEach((header, index) => {
    if (!header || header.toString().trim() === '') return;

    let value = rowData[index];
    const cleanHeader = header.toString().toLowerCase().trim();

    if (value === '' || value === undefined || value === null) {
      value = null;
    }

    if (sheetName === 'Data_Murid' && invalidColumnsForMurid.includes(cleanHeader)) {
      return;
    }

    if ((cleanHeader === 'id' || cleanHeader.includes('_id')) && value) {
      whereCondition[header] = value;
      primaryKeyFound = true;
    } else if (!primaryKeyFound && (cleanHeader.includes('email') || cleanHeader.includes('nis') || cleanHeader.includes('nik')) && value) {
      whereCondition[header] = value;
    } else if (!['created_at', 'updated_at', 'timestamp', 'foto', 'foto_profil'].includes(cleanHeader)) {
      updateData[header] = value;
    }
  });

  if (!primaryKeyFound && Object.keys(updateData).length > 0) {
    const uniqueFields = ['email', 'nis', 'nik', 'nama', 'no_hp'];
    for (const field of uniqueFields) {
      const fieldIndex = headers.findIndex(h => h.toString().toLowerCase().includes(field));
      if (fieldIndex !== -1 && rowData[fieldIndex]) {
        whereCondition[headers[fieldIndex]] = rowData[fieldIndex];
        primaryKeyFound = true;
        break;
      }
    }
  }

  Logger.log(`🔧 Prepared data for ${sheetName}:`);
  Logger.log(`   Where: ${JSON.stringify(whereCondition)}`);
  Logger.log(`   Update: ${JSON.stringify(updateData)}`);

  return {
    updateData: updateData,
    whereCondition: whereCondition,
    isValid: primaryKeyFound && Object.keys(updateData).length > 0,
    error: !primaryKeyFound ? 'Tidak ditemukan primary key yang valid' : 
           Object.keys(updateData).length === 0 ? 'Tidak ada data yang akan diupdate' : null
  };
}

function prepareDataForUpdateFlexible(headers, rowData, sheetName) {
  try {
    console.log(`🔧 Preparing flexible data for ${sheetName}...`);
    
    const updateData = {};
    const whereCondition = {};
    let hasValidId = false;
    
    const validation = validateRowDataFlexibleImproved(headers, rowData);
    
    if (!validation.isValid) {
      console.log(`❌ Data tidak valid: ${validation.errors.join(', ')}`);
      return { 
        isValid: false, 
        error: validation.errors.join(', '),
        updateData: {},
        whereCondition: {}
      };
    }
    
    headers.forEach((header, index) => {
      if (!header || header.toString().trim() === '') return;
      
      const value = rowData[index];
      const cleanHeader = header.toString().toLowerCase().trim();
      
      if (value === '' || value === undefined || value === null) {
        return;
      }
      
      if ((cleanHeader === 'id' || cleanHeader.includes('_id')) && value) {
        whereCondition[header] = value;
        hasValidId = true;
      } else if (!['created_at', 'updated_at', 'timestamp'].includes(cleanHeader)) {
        updateData[header] = value;
      }
    });
    
    if (!hasValidId && validation.hasValidId) {
      hasValidId = true;
    }
    
    return {
      isValid: hasValidId && Object.keys(updateData).length > 0,
      updateData: updateData,
      whereCondition: whereCondition,
      error: !hasValidId ? 'Tidak ditemukan ID yang valid' : 
             Object.keys(updateData).length === 0 ? 'Tidak ada data untuk diupdate' : null
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(`❌ Error prepare flexible: ${error.toString()}`);
    return { 
      isValid: false, 
      error: error.toString(),
      updateData: {},
      whereCondition: {}
    };
  }
}

function prepareDataForUpdateStrict(headers, rowData, sheetName) {
  try {
    console.log(`🔧 Preparing strict data for ${sheetName}...`);
    
    const updateData = {};
    const whereCondition = {};
    let hasId = false;
    
    const validation = validateRowDataStrict(headers, rowData);
    
    if (!validation.isValid) {
      console.log(`❌ Data tidak valid secara strict: ${validation.errors.join(', ')}`);
      return { 
        isValid: false, 
        error: validation.errors.join(', '),
        updateData: {},
        whereCondition: {}
      };
    }
    
    headers.forEach((header, index) => {
      if (!header || header.toString().trim() === '') return;
      
      const value = rowData[index];
      const cleanHeader = header.toString().toLowerCase().trim();
      
      if ((cleanHeader === 'id' || cleanHeader.includes('_id')) && value) {
        whereCondition[header] = value;
        hasId = true;
      } else if (!['created_at', 'updated_at', 'timestamp'].includes(cleanHeader)) {
        updateData[header] = value;
      }
    });
    
    return {
      isValid: hasId && Object.keys(updateData).length > 0,
      updateData: updateData,
      whereCondition: whereCondition,
      error: !hasId ? 'ID tidak ditemukan' : 
             Object.keys(updateData).length === 0 ? 'Tidak ada data untuk diupdate' : null
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(`❌ Error prepare strict: ${error.toString()}`);
    return { 
      isValid: false, 
      error: error.toString(),
      updateData: {},
      whereCondition: {}
    };
  }
}

function prepareDataForUpdateSimple(headers, rowData, sheetName) {
  try {
    console.log(`🔧 Preparing simple data for ${sheetName}...`);
    
    const updateData = {};
    const whereCondition = {};
    
    const tableName = getTableName(sheetName);
    const primaryKey = getPrimaryKeyForTable(tableName);
    const pkIndex = headers.findIndex(h => 
      h && h.toString().toLowerCase().trim() === primaryKey.toLowerCase()
    );
    
    if (pkIndex === -1 || !rowData[pkIndex]) {
      return { 
        isValid: false, 
        error: `Primary key (${primaryKey}) tidak ditemukan`,
        updateData: {},
        whereCondition: {}
      };
    }
    
    whereCondition[headers[pkIndex]] = rowData[pkIndex];
    
    headers.forEach((header, index) => {
      if (!header || header.toString().trim() === '') return;
      
      const value = rowData[index];
      const cleanHeader = header.toString().toLowerCase().trim();
      
      if (value === '' || value === undefined || value === null) {
        return;
      }
      
      if (cleanHeader === primaryKey.toLowerCase()) {
        return; // Skip primary key for update data
      }
      
      if (!['created_at', 'updated_at', 'timestamp'].includes(cleanHeader)) {
        updateData[header] = value;
      }
    });
    
    return {
      isValid: true,
      updateData: updateData,
      whereCondition: whereCondition,
      error: Object.keys(updateData).length === 0 ? 'Tidak ada data untuk diupdate' : null
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(`❌ Error prepare simple: ${error.toString()}`);
    return { 
      isValid: false, 
      error: error.toString(),
      updateData: {},
      whereCondition: {}
    };
  }
}

function validateRowDataFlexibleImproved(headers, rowData) {
  const errors = [];
  let hasValidId = false;
  
  for (let i = 0; i < headers.length; i++) {
    const header = headers[i];
    const value = rowData[i];
    
    if (!header || header.toString().trim() === '') continue;
    
    const cleanHeader = header.toString().toLowerCase().trim();
    
    if ((cleanHeader === 'id' || cleanHeader.includes('_id')) && value) {
      if (value !== '' && value !== null && value !== undefined) {
        hasValidId = true;
      }
    }
    
    if ((cleanHeader.includes('nik') || cleanHeader.includes('nis') || cleanHeader.includes('nip')) && value) {
      const strValue = value.toString().trim();
      if (strValue !== '' && !/^\d+$/.test(strValue)) {
        errors.push(`${header} harus numerik (ditemukan: ${strValue})`);
      }
    }
  }
  
  if (!hasValidId) {
    for (let i = 0; i < headers.length; i++) {
      const header = headers[i].toString().toLowerCase();
      if ((header.includes('email') || header.includes('nama')) && rowData[i]) {
        hasValidId = true;
        break;
      }
    }
    
    if (!hasValidId) {
      errors.push('Tidak ditemukan ID atau identifier yang valid');
    }
  }
  
  return {
    isValid: errors.length === 0,
    errors: errors,
    hasValidId: hasValidId
  };
}

function validateRowDataStrict(headers, rowData) {
  const errors = [];
  let hasId = false;
  
  headers.forEach((header, index) => {
    if (!header) return;
    
    const value = rowData[index];
    const cleanHeader = header.toString().toLowerCase().trim();
    
    if ((cleanHeader === 'id' || cleanHeader.includes('_id')) && value) {
      hasId = true;
    }
    
    if ((cleanHeader.includes('nik') || cleanHeader.includes('nis') || cleanHeader.includes('nip')) && value) {
      const strValue = value.toString().trim();
      if (strValue !== '' && !/^\d+$/.test(strValue)) {
        errors.push(`${header} harus angka (ditemukan: ${strValue})`);
      }
    }
    
    if (cleanHeader.includes('nama') && (!value || value.toString().trim() === '')) {
      errors.push(`${header} tidak boleh kosong`);
    }
  });
  
  if (!hasId) {
    errors.push('ID tidak ditemukan atau kosong');
  }
  
  return {
    isValid: errors.length === 0 && hasId,
    errors: errors,
    hasId: hasId
  };
}

function pushSheetDataDirect(sheetName) {
  try {
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(sheetName);
    if (!sheet) {
      return { success: false, error: 'Sheet tidak ditemukan', successCount: 0, errorCount: 1, skippedCount: 0 };
    }
    
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0];
    
    if (data.length <= 1) {
      return { success: true, message: 'Tidak ada data', successCount: 0, errorCount: 0, skippedCount: 0 };
    }
    
    let successCount = 0, errorCount = 0, skippedCount = 0;
    
    Logger.log(`🔄 ${sheetName}: Processing ${data.length-1} rows secara langsung`);
    
    const batchSize = 20;
    const totalBatches = Math.ceil((data.length - 1) / batchSize);
    
    for (let batch = 0; batch < totalBatches; batch++) {
      const startRow = batch * batchSize + 1;
      const endRow = Math.min(startRow + batchSize, data.length);
      
      if (batch % 10 === 0) {
        Logger.log(`🔄 Batch ${batch+1}/${totalBatches}: Baris ${startRow}-${endRow-1}`);
      }
      
      for (let i = startRow; i < endRow; i++) {
        const rowData = data[i];
        
        if (isRowEmpty(rowData)) {
          skippedCount++;
          continue;
        }
        
        const preparation = prepareDataDirect(headers, rowData, sheetName);
        
        if (!preparation.isValid) {
          skippedCount++;
          continue;
        }
        
        try {
          const result = updateDataToMySQL(
            getTableName(sheetName), 
            preparation.updateData, 
            preparation.whereCondition
          );
          
          if (result && result.success) {
            successCount++;
          } else if (result && result.skipped) {
            skippedCount++;
          } else {
            errorCount++;
          }
          
        } catch (error) {
          errorCount++;
          if (errorCount <= 5) {
            Logger.log(`❌ Error baris ${i+1}: ${error.toString().substring(0, 100)}`);
          }
        }
      }
    }
    
    Logger.log(`📊 ${sheetName}: ${successCount}✅ ${errorCount}❌ ${skippedCount}⏩`);
    
    return {
      success: errorCount === 0,
      successCount, errorCount, skippedCount,
      totalProcessed: successCount + errorCount + skippedCount
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    Logger.log(`❌ Direct processing failed: ${error.toString()}`);
    return {
      success: false,
      error: error.toString(),
      successCount: 0, errorCount: 1, skippedCount: 0
    };
  }
}

// function pushSheetDataDirectSimple(sheetName, maxRows = 5) {
//   try {
//     const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(sheetName);
//     if (!sheet) {
//       return { success: false, error: 'Sheet tidak ditemukan', successCount: 0, errorCount: 1, skippedCount: 0 };
//     }
