          }
        }
        
        /* Quick Filter Buttons */
        .quick-filters {
          display: flex;
          gap: 10px;
          margin-top: 15px;
          flex-wrap: wrap;
        }
        
        .filter-btn {
          padding: 8px 16px;
          background: white;
          border: 2px solid #dee2e6;
          border-radius: 8px;
          cursor: pointer;
          font-size: 14px;
          font-weight: 500;
          color: #495057;
          transition: all 0.2s ease;
        }
        
        .filter-btn:hover {
          border-color: #4CAF50;
          color: #4CAF50;
        }
        
        .filter-btn.active {
          background: #4CAF50;
          color: white;
          border-color: #4CAF50;
        }
      </style>
    </head>
    <body>
      <div class="container">
        <div class="header">
          <h1>🎓 Pindahkan Murid ke Alumni</h1>
          <div class="header-subtitle">Pilih murid yang akan dipindahkan ke data alumni</div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="content">
          <!-- Search Section -->
          <div class="search-section">
            <div class="search-container">
              <div class="search-box">
                <span class="search-icon">🔍</span>
                <input type="text" 
                       id="searchInput" 
                       class="search-input" 
                       placeholder="Cari berdasarkan nama, NIS, kelas, atau kamar..."
                       autocomplete="off">
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <div class="quick-filters">
              <button class="filter-btn active" onclick="filterByStatus('all')">Semua</button>
              <button class="filter-btn" onclick="filterByStatus('selected')">Terpilih</button>
              <button class="filter-btn" onclick="filterByStatus('unselected')">Belum Dipilih</button>
              <button class="filter-btn" onclick="filterByStatus('with_kelas')">Ada Kelas</button>
              <button class="filter-btn" onclick="filterByStatus('with_kamar')">Ada Kamar</button>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <!-- Stats -->
          <div class="stats-container">
            <div class="stat-card">
              <div class="stat-value" id="totalStudents">0</div>
              <div class="stat-label">Total Murid</div>
            </div>
            <div class="stat-card">
              <div class="stat-value" id="selectedStudents">0</div>
              <div class="stat-label">Terpilih</div>
            </div>
            <div class="stat-card">
              <div class="stat-value" id="filteredStudents">0</div>
              <div class="stat-label">Tampil</div>
            </div>
            <div class="stat-card">
              <div class="stat-value" id="availableStudents">0</div>
              <div class="stat-label">Tersedia</div>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <!-- Student List -->
          <div class="student-list-container">
            <div class="list-header">
              <div>Pilih</div>
              <div>Nama Murid</div>
              <div>NIS</div>
              <div>Kelas</div>
              <div>Kamar</div>
            </div>
            <div class="student-list" id="studentList">
              <!-- Data akan diisi oleh JavaScript -->
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <!-- Config Section -->
          <div class="config-section">
            <div class="form-group">
              <label class="form-label" for="statusKeluar">Status Keluar:</label>
              <select id="statusKeluar" class="form-select">
                <option value="Lulus">Lulus</option>
                <option value="Pindah">Pindah</option>
                <option value="Berhenti">Berhenti</option>
                <option value="Dikeluarkan">Dikeluarkan</option>
              </select>
            </div>
            
            <div class="form-group">
              <label class="form-label" for="keterangan">Keterangan (Opsional):</label>
              <textarea id="keterangan" class="form-textarea" placeholder="Masukkan keterangan tambahan..."></textarea>
            </div>
            
            <div class="form-group">
              <label class="form-label">Tahun Keluar:</label>
              <input type="number" id="tahunKeluar" class="form-input" 
                     value="${new Date().getFullYear()}" 
                     min="2000" max="${new Date().getFullYear() + 5}">
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <!-- Action Buttons -->
          <div class="action-section">
            <div class="selection-info">
              Murid terpilih: <span class="selected-count" id="selectedCount">0</span> dari <span id="totalCount">0</span> murid
            </div>
            <div class="action-buttons">
              <button class="btn btn-cancel" onclick="google.script.host.close()">
                <span>✕</span> Batal
              </button>
              <button class="btn btn-submit" id="submitBtn" onclick="processSelection()">
                <span>🚀</span> Proses ke Alumni
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <!-- Loading Overlay -->
      <div class="loading-overlay" id="loadingOverlay">
        <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
        <div class="loading-text">Memproses data...</div>
      </div>
      
      <script>
        let allStudents = ${muridListJson};
        let filteredStudents = [];
        let selectedIds = new Set();
        let currentFilter = 'all';
        let searchTimeout = null;
        
        // Initialize
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
          console.log('Form dimuat dengan ' + allStudents.length + ' data murid');
          renderStudentList();
          updateStats();
          
          // Setup search dengan debounce untuk responsif
          const searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
          if (searchInput) {
            searchInput.addEventListener('input', function(e) {
              clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
              searchTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
                console.log('Pencarian dilakukan: ' + e.target.value);
                renderStudentList();
              }, 300); // Debounce 300ms
            });
            
            // Juga trigger pada Enter
            searchInput.addEventListener('keypress', function(e) {
              if (e.key === 'Enter') {
                clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
                renderStudentList();
              }
            });
          }
          
          // Enable/disable submit button based on selection
          setInterval(() => {
            const submitBtn = document.getElementById('submitBtn');
            if (submitBtn) {
              submitBtn.disabled = selectedIds.size === 0;
            }
          }, 500);
        });
        
        // Render student list
        function renderStudentList() {
          const container = document.getElementById('studentList');
          const searchTerm = document.getElementById('searchInput') ? 
                            document.getElementById('searchInput').value.toLowerCase().trim() : '';
          
          // Filter students berdasarkan pencarian
          filteredStudents = allStudents.filter(student => {
            // Apply text search
            if (searchTerm) {
              const searchableText = [
                student.nama?.toString().toLowerCase() || '',
                student.nis?.toString().toLowerCase() || '',
                student.kelas?.toString().toLowerCase() || '',
                student.kamar?.toString().toLowerCase() || '',
                student.id?.toString().toLowerCase() || ''
              ].join(' ');
              
              if (!searchableText.includes(searchTerm)) {
                return false;
              }
            }
            
            // Apply status filter
            const isSelected = selectedIds.has(student.id.toString());
            switch (currentFilter) {
              case 'selected':
                return isSelected;
              case 'unselected':
                return !isSelected;
              case 'with_kelas':
                return student.kelas && student.kelas.trim() !== '' && student.kelas !== '-';
              case 'with_kamar':
                return student.kamar && student.kamar.trim() !== '' && student.kamar !== '-';
              case 'all':
              default:
                return true;
            }
          });
          
          console.log('Tampilkan ' + filteredStudents.length + ' dari ' + allStudents.length + ' murid');
          
          // Generate HTML
          let html = '';
          
          if (filteredStudents.length === 0) {
            html = \`
              <div class="no-results">
                <span class="no-results-icon">📭</span>
                <h3>Tidak ada data murid</h3>
                <p>\${searchTerm ? 'Tidak ditemukan murid dengan kata kunci: "' + searchTerm + '"' : 'Tidak ditemukan data murid yang sesuai filter'}</p>
              </div>
            \`;
          } else {
            filteredStudents.forEach((student, index) => {
              const isSelected = selectedIds.has(student.id.toString());
              const rowClass = isSelected ? 'student-item selected' : 'student-item';
              
              html += \`
                <div class="\${rowClass}" onclick="toggleSelection('\${student.id}', event)">
                  <div>
                    <input type="checkbox" 
                           class="student-checkbox"
                           value="\${student.id}"
                           \${isSelected ? 'checked' : ''}
                           onclick="event.stopPropagation(); toggleSelection('\${student.id}', event)">
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <div class="student-name">\${escapeHtml(student.nama || 'Tidak ada nama')}</div>
                    <div class="student-id">ID: \${student.id}</div>
                  </div>
                  <div class="student-detail">
                    \${escapeHtml(student.nis || '-')}
                  </div>
                  <div class="student-detail">
                    \${escapeHtml(student.kelas || '-')}
                    <small>Kelas</small>
                  </div>
                  <div class="student-detail">
                    \${escapeHtml(student.kamar || '-')}
                    <small>Kamar</small>
                  </div>
                </div>
              \`;
            });
          }
          
          container.innerHTML = html;
          updateStats();
        }
        
        // Helper function untuk escape HTML
        function escapeHtml(text) {
          if (!text) return '';
          return text
            .toString()
            .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
            .replace(/</g, "&lt;")
            .replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
            .replace(/"/g, "&quot;")
            .replace(/'/g, "&#039;");
        }
        
        // Filter by status
        function filterByStatus(status) {
          // Update button states
          document.querySelectorAll('.filter-btn').forEach(btn => {
            btn.classList.remove('active');
          });
          event.target.classList.add('active');
          
          currentFilter = status;
          renderStudentList();
        }
        
        // Filter and render with search
        function filterAndRender() {
          renderStudentList();
        }
        
        // Toggle selection
        function toggleSelection(studentId, event) {
          if (event) {
            event.stopPropagation();
          }
          
          if (selectedIds.has(studentId)) {
            selectedIds.delete(studentId);
          } else {
            selectedIds.add(studentId);
          }
          
          // Update UI langsung tanpa render ulang seluruh list
          const item = event ? event.currentTarget : document.querySelector(\`.student-item input[value="\${studentId}"]\`)?.closest('.student-item');
          if (item) {
            if (selectedIds.has(studentId)) {
              item.classList.add('selected');
              item.querySelector('.student-checkbox').checked = true;
            } else {
              item.classList.remove('selected');
              item.querySelector('.student-checkbox').checked = false;
            }
          }
          
          updateStats();
        }
        
        // Select all visible
        function selectAllVisible() {
          filteredStudents.forEach(student => {
            selectedIds.add(student.id.toString());
          });
          renderStudentList();
        }
        
        // Deselect all
        function deselectAll() {
          selectedIds.clear();
          renderStudentList();
        }
        
        // Update statistics
        function updateStats() {
          const total = allStudents.length;
          const selected = selectedIds.size;
          const filtered = filteredStudents.length;
          const available = total - selected;
          
          document.getElementById('totalStudents').textContent = total;
          document.getElementById('selectedStudents').textContent = selected;
          document.getElementById('filteredStudents').textContent = filtered;
          document.getElementById('availableStudents').textContent = available;
          document.getElementById('selectedCount').textContent = selected;
          document.getElementById('totalCount').textContent = total;
        }
        
        // Process selection
        function processSelection() {
          const selectedIdsArray = Array.from(selectedIds);
          
          if (selectedIdsArray.length === 0) {
            alert('Silakan pilih minimal satu murid untuk dipindahkan ke alumni.');
            return;
          }
          
          const statusKeluar = document.getElementById('statusKeluar').value;
          const keterangan = document.getElementById('keterangan').value;
          const tahunKeluar = document.getElementById('tahunKeluar').value;
          
          // Validation
          if (!statusKeluar) {
            alert('Silakan pilih status keluar.');
            return;
          }
          
          if (!tahunKeluar || tahunKeluar < 2000 || tahunKeluar > new Date().getFullYear() + 5) {
            alert('Tahun keluar tidak valid. Harus antara 2000 dan ' + (new Date().getFullYear() + 5));
            return;
          }
          
          // Show nama murid yang dipilih
          const selectedNames = selectedIdsArray.map(id => {
            const student = allStudents.find(s => s.id.toString() === id.toString());
            return student ? student.nama : 'ID ' + id;
          }).slice(0, 10); // Limit 10 nama
          
          const confirmationMessage = \`Anda akan memindahkan \${selectedIdsArray.length} murid ke alumni:\\n\\n\` +
            selectedNames.map(name => \`• \${name}\`).join('\\n') +
            (selectedIdsArray.length > 10 ? \`\\n...dan \${selectedIdsArray.length - 10} lainnya\\n\\n\` : '\\n\\n') +
            \`Status: "\${statusKeluar}"\\n\` +
            \`Tahun Keluar: \${tahunKeluar}\\n\\n\` +
            \`Lanjutkan?\`;
          
          if (!confirm(confirmationMessage)) {
            return;
          }
          
          // Show loading
          document.getElementById('loadingOverlay').style.display = 'flex';
          
          // Send to server
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
              document.getElementById('loadingOverlay').style.display = 'none';
              
              if (result.success) {
                const message = \`✅ Berhasil memindahkan \${result.successCount} murid ke alumni\\n\` +
                               \`❌ Gagal: \${result.errorCount || 0} murid\\n\` +
                               \`📊 Total diproses: \${result.totalProcessed || 0}\`;
                
                alert(message);
                
                // Close dialog on success
                if (result.successCount > 0) {
                  setTimeout(() => {
                    google.script.host.close();
                  }, 1000);
                }
              } else {
                alert(\`❌ Gagal: \${result.message || 'Terjadi kesalahan'}\`);
              }
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(error) {
              document.getElementById('loadingOverlay').style.display = 'none';
              alert(\`❌ Error: \${error.message || 'Terjadi kesalahan pada server'}\`);
            })
            .prosesPindahKeAlumni(selectedIdsArray, statusKeluar, keterangan, parseInt(tahunKeluar));
        }
        
        // Keyboard shortcuts
        document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
          // Ctrl/Cmd + A to select all visible
          if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'a') {
            e.preventDefault();
            selectAllVisible();
          }
          
          // Escape to deselect all
          if (e.key === 'Escape') {
            deselectAll();
          }
          
          // Ctrl/Cmd + Enter to submit
          if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'Enter') {
            e.preventDefault();
            if (selectedIds.size > 0) {
              processSelection();
            }
          }
          
          // Fokus pada search input saat tekan /
          if (e.key === '/' && e.target.tagName !== 'INPUT' && e.target.tagName !== 'TEXTAREA') {
            e.preventDefault();
            const searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
            if (searchInput) {
              searchInput.focus();
            }
          }
        });
        
        // Highlight search matches
        function highlightSearchMatches() {
          const searchTerm = document.getElementById('searchInput').value.toLowerCase();
          if (!searchTerm) return;
          
          const items = document.querySelectorAll('.student-item');
          items.forEach(item => {
            const text = item.textContent.toLowerCase();
            if (text.includes(searchTerm)) {
              item.style.backgroundColor = '#fff9c4'; // Highlight color
            } else {
              item.style.backgroundColor = '';
            }
          });
        }
        
        // Clear search
        function clearSearch() {
          document.getElementById('searchInput').value = '';
          renderStudentList();
        }
      </script>
    </body>
    </html>
  `;
}

// Fungsi bantu untuk mencari murid yang cocok dengan kriteria pencarian
function searchMuridForAlumni(searchTerm) {
  try {
    const spreadsheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const muridSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName('Data_Murid');
    
    if (!muridSheet || muridSheet.getLastRow() <= 1) {
      return [];
    }
    
    const data = muridSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0];
    
    const idIndex = headers.indexOf('murid_id');
    const namaIndex = headers.indexOf('nama');
    const nisIndex = headers.indexOf('nis');
    const kelasIndex = headers.indexOf('kelas_madin_id');
    const kamarIndex = headers.indexOf('kamar_id');
    
    if (idIndex === -1 || namaIndex === -1) {
      return [];
    }
    
    const refData = getReferensiData();
    const results = [];
    
    const searchLower = searchTerm.toLowerCase();
    
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      const muridId = data[i][idIndex];
      const nama = data[i][namaIndex] || '';
      const nis = data[i][nisIndex] || '';
      const kelasId = data[i][kelasIndex] || '';
      const kamarId = data[i][kamarIndex] || '';
      
      let keteranganKelas = '';
      let keteranganKamar = '';
      
      if (kelasId && refData.kelas_madin_id && refData.kelas_madin_id[kelasId]) {
        keteranganKelas = refData.kelas_madin_id[kelasId];
      }
      
      if (kamarId && refData.kamar_id && refData.kamar_id[kamarId]) {
        keteranganKamar = refData.kamar_id[kamarId];
      }
      
      // Check if any field contains the search term
      const matches = nama.toLowerCase().includes(searchLower) ||
                     nis.toLowerCase().includes(searchLower) ||
                     keteranganKelas.toLowerCase().includes(searchLower) ||
                     keteranganKamar.toLowerCase().includes(searchLower) ||
                     muridId.toString().includes(searchTerm);
      
      if (matches && muridId) {
        results.push({
          id: muridId,
          nama: nama,
          nis: nis,
          kelas: keteranganKelas,
          kamar: keteranganKamar
        });
      }
    }
    
    return results;
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(`❌ Error searchMuridForAlumni: ${error.toString()}`);
    return [];
  }
}

// Fungsi untuk membuat form pencarian yang lebih baik
function createImprovedSearchForm() {
  try {
    console.log('🔍 Membuat form pencarian yang lebih baik...');
    
    const spreadsheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const muridSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName('Data_Murid');
    
    if (!muridSheet || muridSheet.getLastRow() <= 1) {
      return 'Tidak ada data murid';
    }
    
    const data = muridSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const headers = data[0];
    
    // Ambil SEMUA data murid
    const muridList = [];
    const refData = getReferensiData();
    
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      try {
        const muridId = data[i][headers.indexOf('murid_id')];
        const nama = data[i][headers.indexOf('nama')] || '';
        
        if (muridId && nama) {
          muridList.push({
            id: muridId,
            nama: nama,
            nis: data[i][headers.indexOf('nis')] || '',
            kelas: refData.kelas_madin_id && muridId ? 
                   refData.kelas_madin_id[data[i][headers.indexOf('kelas_madin_id')]] || '' : '',
            kamar: refData.kamar_id && muridId ? 
                   refData.kamar_id[data[i][headers.indexOf('kamar_id')]] || '' : ''
          });
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.error(`Error memproses baris ${i}: ${e}`);
      }
    }
    
    console.log(`📊 Data murid siap: ${muridList.length} entri`);
    
    // Buat HTML dengan fitur pencarian yang lebih baik
    return createEnhancedSearchHTML(muridList);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(`❌ Error createImprovedSearchForm: ${error.toString()}`);
    return `<h3>Error: ${error.toString()}</h3>`;
  }
}

// Fungsi untuk membuat HTML dengan pencarian yang lebih baik
function createEnhancedSearchHTML(muridList) {
  const muridListJson = JSON.stringify(muridList);
  
  return `
    <!DOCTYPE html>
    <html>
    <head>
      <base target="_top">
      <meta charset="UTF-8">
      <style>
        body {
          font-family: Arial, sans-serif;
          margin: 20px;
          max-width: 1000px;
          margin: 0 auto;
        }
        
        .search-container {
          margin: 20px 0;
          padding: 20px;
          background: #f5f5f5;
          border-radius: 10px;
        }
        
        .search-box {
          display: flex;
          gap: 10px;
          margin-bottom: 15px;
        }
        
        .search-input {
          flex: 1;
          padding: 12px;
          border: 2px solid #ddd;
          border-radius: 5px;
          font-size: 16px;
        }
        
        .search-btn {
          padding: 12px 24px;
          background: #4CAF50;
          color: white;
          border: none;
          border-radius: 5px;
          cursor: pointer;
        }
        
        .search-btn:hover {
          background: #45a049;
        }
        
        .search-stats {
          font-size: 14px;
          color: #666;
          margin-top: 10px;
        }
        
        .results-container {
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow-y: auto;
          border: 1px solid #ddd;
          border-radius: 5px;
          margin: 20px 0;
        }
        
        .result-item {
          padding: 15px;
          border-bottom: 1px solid #eee;
          display: flex;
          align-items: center;
          gap: 15px;
        }
        
        .result-item:hover {
          background: #f9f9f9;
        }
        
        .result-checkbox {
          width: 20px;
          height: 20px;
        }
        
        .result-info {
          flex: 1;
        }
        
        .result-name {
          font-weight: bold;
          font-size: 16px;
        }
        
        .result-details {
          font-size: 14px;
          color: #666;
          margin-top: 5px;
        }
        
        .highlight {
          background-color: yellow;
          font-weight: bold;
        }
        
        .loading {
          text-align: center;
          padding: 20px;
          color: #666;
        }
      </style>
    </head>
    <body>
      <h2>🎓 Pilih Murid untuk Alumni</h2>
      
      <div class="search-container">
        <div class="search-box">
          <input type="text" 
                 id="searchInput" 
                 class="search-input" 
                 placeholder="Cari nama, NIS, kelas, atau kamar..."
                 autocomplete="off">
          <button class="search-btn" onclick="performSearch()">Cari</button>
        </div>
        <div class="search-stats">
          Menampilkan <span id="resultCount">0</span> dari <span id="totalCount">${muridList.length}</span> murid
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <div class="results-container" id="resultsContainer">
        <div class="loading" id="loading">Memuat data...</div>
      </div>
      
      <script>
        const allMurid = ${muridListJson};
        let selectedIds = new Set();
        let currentSearch = '';
        
        // Initialize
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
          console.log('Total murid:', allMurid.length);
          performSearch();
          
          // Setup instant search
          const searchInput = document.getElementById('searchInput');
          let searchTimeout;
          
          searchInput.addEventListener('input', function(e) {
            clearTimeout(searchTimeout);
            searchTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
              currentSearch = e.target.value.trim().toLowerCase();
              performSearch();
            }, 300);
          });
          
          // Focus on search input
          searchInput.focus();
        });
        
        function performSearch() {
          const searchTerm = document.getElementById('searchInput').value.trim().toLowerCase();
          currentSearch = searchTerm;
          
          const container = document.getElementById('resultsContainer');
          
          if (!searchTerm) {
            // Tampilkan semua data jika pencarian kosong
            displayResults(allMurid);
            return;
          }
          
          // Filter data
          const filtered = allMurid.filter(murid => {
            const searchText = \`
              \${murid.nama || ''}
              \${murid.nis || ''}
              \${murid.kelas || ''}
              \${murid.kamar || ''}
              \${murid.id || ''}
            \`.toLowerCase();
            
            return searchText.includes(searchTerm);
          });
          
          displayResults(filtered);
        }
        
        function displayResults(results) {
          const container = document.getElementById('resultsContainer');
          const searchTerm = currentSearch;
          
          if (results.length === 0) {
            container.innerHTML = \`
              <div class="loading">
                <p>Tidak ditemukan murid yang cocok dengan pencarian: "\${searchTerm}"</p>
                <p>Coba gunakan kata kunci yang berbeda</p>
              </div>
            \`;
            updateStats(results.length);
            return;
          }
          
          let html = '';
          
          results.forEach(murid => {
            const isSelected = selectedIds.has(murid.id.toString());
            
            // Highlight search term in results
            const highlightText = (text) => {
              if (!text || !searchTerm) return text || '';
              const regex = new RegExp(\`(\${searchTerm.replace(/[.*+?^${'$'}{}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&')})\`, 'gi');
              return text.toString().replace(regex, '<span class="highlight">$1</span>');
            };
            
            html += \`
              <div class="result-item">
                <input type="checkbox" 
                       class="result-checkbox"
                       value="\${murid.id}"
                       \${isSelected ? 'checked' : ''}
                       onchange="toggleSelection('\${murid.id}')">
                <div class="result-info">
                  <div class="result-name">\${highlightText(murid.nama)}</div>
                  <div class="result-details">
                    ID: \${murid.id} | 
                    NIS: \${highlightText(murid.nis || '-')} | 
                    Kelas: \${highlightText(murid.kelas || '-')} | 
                    Kamar: \${highlightText(murid.kamar || '-')}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            \`;
          });
          
          container.innerHTML = html;
          updateStats(results.length);
        }
        
        function toggleSelection(muridId) {
          if (selectedIds.has(muridId)) {
            selectedIds.delete(muridId);
          } else {
            selectedIds.add(muridId);
          }
          
          // Update UI
          const checkbox = document.querySelector(\`.result-checkbox[value="\${muridId}"]\`);
          if (checkbox) {
            checkbox.checked = selectedIds.has(muridId);
          }
        }
        
        function updateStats(count) {
          document.getElementById('resultCount').textContent = count;
          document.getElementById('totalCount').textContent = allMurid.length;
        }
        
        // Keyboard shortcuts
        document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
          // Ctrl/Cmd + F to focus search
          if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.key === 'f') {
            e.preventDefault();
            document.getElementById('searchInput').focus();
          }
        });
      </script>
    </body>
    </html>
  `;
}

// =============================================
// 17. FUNGSI LOGGING ENHANCED
// =============================================
function setLogLevel(level) {
  CURRENT_LOG_LEVEL = level;
}

function logDebug(message) {
  if (CURRENT_LOG_LEVEL <= LOG_LEVELS.DEBUG) {
    Logger.log(`🔍 [DEBUG] ${message}`);
  }
}

function logInfo(message) {
  if (CURRENT_LOG_LEVEL <= LOG_LEVELS.INFO) {
    Logger.log(`ℹ️ [INFO] ${message}`);
  }
}

function logWarn(message) {
  if (CURRENT_LOG_LEVEL <= LOG_LEVELS.WARN) {
    Logger.log(`⚠️ [WARN] ${message}`);
  }
}

function logError(message, error = null) {
  if (CURRENT_LOG_LEVEL <= LOG_LEVELS.ERROR) {
    const errorMsg = error ? `${message}: ${error.toString()}` : message;
    Logger.log(`❌ [ERROR] ${errorMsg}`);
    
    if (error && error.toString().includes('critical')) {
      SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().toast(
        message,
        'Critical Error',
        10
      );
    }
  }
}

function logAlumniActivity(action, details) {
  const logSheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet()
    .getSheetByName('LOG_ALUMNI') || buatSheet('LOG_ALUMNI');
  
  const timestamp = new Date();
  logSheet.appendRow([timestamp, action, JSON.stringify(details)]);
}

// EXECUTION MONITOR (TAMBAHKAN SEBAGAI BAGIAN BARU)
function safeExecuteWithTimeout(func, funcName, timeoutMs = 300000) { // 5 menit
  const startTime = new Date().getTime();
  
  try {
    console.log(`⏱️ Executing ${funcName} with ${timeoutMs}ms timeout`);
    const result = func();
    
    const elapsed = new Date().getTime() - startTime;
    console.log(`✅ ${funcName} completed in ${elapsed}ms`);
    
    return result;
  } catch (error) {
    const elapsed = new Date().getTime() - startTime;
    console.error(`❌ ${funcName} failed after ${elapsed}ms: ${error}`);
    
    // Simpan state jika timeout
    if (error.toString().includes('timeout') || elapsed > timeoutMs) {
      console.log(`💾 Saving execution state for ${funcName}`);
      // Implementasi state saving sesuai kebutuhan
    }
    
    throw error;
  }
}

// Wrapper untuk fungsi-fungsi kritis
function safeSyncDataMurid() {
  return safeExecuteWithTimeout(
    () => syncDataMuridWithNotesEnhancedAmanChunked(10),
    'syncDataMurid',
    240000 // 4 menit timeout
  );
}

function safePushAllData() {
  return safeExecuteWithTimeout(
    pushAllDataChunked,
    'pushAllDataChunked',
    300000 // 5 menit timeout
  );
}

function showHelp() {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  
  const helpMessage = `
📚 **PANDUAN PENGGUNAAN SISTEM PPMA**

**🔄 SYNC DATA:**
1. "Sync Data Murid" - Ambil data dari database ke sheet
2. "Sync Semua Data" - Ambil semua data (murid, guru, users, alumni)
3. "Sync Data Referensi" - Ambil data kelas dan kamar

**📤 PUSH DATA:**
1. "Push Semua Data" - Kirim perubahan di sheet ke database
2. Aktifkan "Auto Sync" untuk sinkron otomatis saat edit

**🛠️ PERBAIKAN:**
1. "Perbaiki Notes" - Isi notes untuk ID kelas/kamar
2. "Quick Check" - Cek kesehatan sistem
3. "Diagnosa Error" - Identifikasi masalah

**💾 BACKUP:**
1. Selalu backup sebelum push data besar
2. Restore jika ada kesalahan

**⚠️ TIPS:**
- Jalankan "Health Check" terlebih dahulu
- Sync data dulu sebelum push
- Cek koneksi API jika ada error

Untuk bantuan lebih lanjut, hubungi administrator sistem.
`;
  
  ui.alert('❓ Bantuan Sistem PPMA', helpMessage, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
}

function sendToApi(payload) {
  try {
    var options = {
      'method': 'post',
      'contentType': 'application/json',
      'payload': JSON.stringify(payload),
      'muteHttpExceptions': true
    };
    
    var response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(API_BASE_URL, options);
    var responseCode = response.getResponseCode();
    var responseText = response.getContentText();
    
    console.log(`📊 Response Code: ${responseCode}`);
    
    if (responseCode === 200) {
      var jsonResponse = JSON.parse(responseText);
      return {
        success: true,
        message: jsonResponse.message || 'Berhasil'
      };
    } else {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: `Error ${responseCode}: ${responseText}`
      };
    }
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('❌ Error sendToApi:', error);
    return {
      success: false,
      message: error.toString()
    };
  }
}

function jalankanSyncLengkap() {
  try {
    console.log('🚀 Memulai sinkronisasi lengkap...');
    
    SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().toast(
      'Memulai sinkronisasi lengkap...',
      'Sync System',
      3
    );
    
    // 1. Sync data referensi terlebih dahulu
    const refResults = syncReferensiData();
    console.log('✅ Referensi data:', refResults);
    
    Utilities.sleep(2000);
    
    // 2. Sync data utama dengan notes
    const muridResult = syncDataMuridWithNotesEnhanced();
    console.log('✅ Data murid:', muridResult);
    
    Utilities.sleep(2000);
    
    // 3. Sync data lainnya
    const results = [];
    
    const syncFunctions = [
      { name: 'Guru', func: syncDataGuruViaAPI },
      { name: 'Users', func: syncDataUsersViaAPI },
      { name: 'Alumni', func: syncDataAlumniViaAPI }
    ];
    
    syncFunctions.forEach(({ name, func }) => {
      try {
        const result = func();
        results.push(`${name}: ${result.includes('SUCCESS') ? '✅' : '❌'}`);
        Utilities.sleep(1500);
      } catch (error) {
        results.push(`${name}: ❌ ${error.toString()}`);
      }
    });
    
    // 4. Setup trigger jika belum ada
    if (!checkEditTrigger()) {
      setupEditTrigger();
      results.push('Trigger: ✅ Diaktifkan');
    }
    
    // 5. Tampilkan hasil
    const summary = `📊 HASIL SYNCRONISASI LENGKAP:\n\n` +
                   `• Referensi: ${refResults.length} sheets\n` +
                   `• Murid: ${muridResult.includes('SUCCESS') ? '✅' : '❌'}\n` +
                   `${results.map(r => `• ${r}`).join('\n')}\n\n` +
                   `Sistem siap digunakan!`;
    
    console.log(summary);
    
    const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
    ui.alert('✅ Sinkronisasi Lengkap Selesai', summary, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    
    return { success: true, results: [muridResult, ...results] };
    
  } catch (error) {
    const errorMsg = `❌ Sync lengkap gagal: ${error.toString()}`;
    console.error(errorMsg);
    
    const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
    ui.alert('❌ Sync Gagal', errorMsg, ui.ButtonSet.OK);
    
    return { success: false, error: errorMsg };
  }
}

// =============================================
// 19. FUNGSI NOTIFIKASI (dipanggil tapi tidak didefinisikan)
// =============================================
function sendHealthAlertEmail(report) {
  try {
    const recipient = Session.getActiveUser().getEmail();
    const timestamp = new Date().toLocaleString();
    
    let subject = `🚨 PPMA System Alert - Health Check Failed`;
    let body = `PPMA SYSTEM HEALTH ALERT\n\n`;
    body += `⚠️ **SYSTEM ISSUES DETECTED**\n\n`;
    body += `Timestamp: ${timestamp}\n`;
    body += `Score: ${report.performance?.score || 0}/100\n`;
    body += `Issues: ${report.issues?.length || 0} total\n\n`;
    
    body += `📋 **ISSUE DETAILS**:\n`;
    if (report.issues && report.issues.length > 0) {
      report.issues.forEach(issue => {
        body += `• ${issue.severity === 'HIGH' ? '🔴' : '🟡'} ${issue.message}\n`;
      });
    }
    
    body += `\n📊 **SYSTEM STATS**:\n`;
    body += `• Success Rate: ${report.statistics?.realtime?.successRate || 0}%\n`;
    body += `• Total Errors: ${report.statistics?.errors?.totalErrors || 0}\n`;
    body += `• Active Triggers: ${report.statistics?.system?.hasEditTrigger ? 'Yes' : 'No'}\n`;
    
    body += `\n🔗 **SPREADSHEET**: ${SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getUrl()}\n`;
    body += `👤 **USER**: ${Session.getActiveUser().getEmail()}\n\n`;
    
    body += `⚠️ This is an automated alert from PPMA Sync System\n`;
    
    MailApp.sendEmail({
      to: recipient,
      subject: subject,
      body: body
    });
    
    console.log(`📧 Health alert email sent to: ${recipient}`);
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(`❌ Failed to send health alert email: ${error.toString()}`);
  }
}

function sendAutoSyncNotification(subject, content) {
  try {
    const recipient = Session.getActiveUser().getEmail();
    const timestamp = new Date().toLocaleString();
    
    let body = `📊 NOTIFIKASI SISTEM PPMA\n\n`;
    body += `Waktu: ${timestamp}\n`;
    body += `User: ${recipient}\n`;
    body += `Spreadsheet: ${SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getName()}\n`;
    body += `\n📋 DETAIL:\n`;
    
    if (typeof content === 'string') {
      body += content;
    } else if (Array.isArray(content)) {
      body += content.join('\n');
    } else {
      body += JSON.stringify(content, null, 2);
    }
    
    body += `\n\n🔗 Link Spreadsheet: ${SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getUrl()}`;
    body += `\n⚠️ Email ini dikirim otomatis oleh sistem PPMA`;
    
    MailApp.sendEmail({
      to: recipient,
      subject: `[PPMA AUTO] ${subject}`,
      body: body
    });
    
    Logger.log(`📧 Notifikasi email terkirim ke: ${recipient}`);
    
  } catch (error) {
    Logger.log(`⚠️ Gagal kirim email: ${error.toString()}`);
  }
}

// =============================================
// 20. FUNGSI SINKRONISASI TABEL BARU AMAN
// =============================================
function syncTabelBaruAman() {
  try {
    console.log('🚀 Memulai sinkronisasi tabel baru dengan metode hybrid...');
    const spreadsheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    
    // Tampilkan dialog pilihan
    const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
    const response = ui.alert(
      'Sinkronisasi Tabel Baru',
      'Pilih metode sinkronisasi:\n\n' +
      '1. ✅ **Metode Aman** (Direkomendasikan)\n' +
      '   - Menggunakan daftar tabel yang sudah dikonfirmasi\n' +
      '   - Endpoint khusus untuk setiap tabel\n' +
      '   - Lebih stabil dan teruji\n\n' +
      '2. 🔍 **Metode Otomatis**\n' +
      '   - Mendeteksi struktur database\n' +
      '   - Untuk tabel-tabel yang belum dikenali\n' +
      '   - Berisiko jika endpoint tidak sesuai',
      ui.ButtonSet.YES_NO_CANCEL
    );
    
    let results;
    
    if (response === ui.Button.YES) {
      // Metode Aman (menggunakan daftar tabel yang sudah dikonfirmasi)
      results = syncTabelTerdefinisi();
    } else if (response === ui.Button.NO) {
      // Metode Otomatis (deteksi struktur)
      results = syncTabelOtomatis();
    } else {
      return 'Dibatalkan oleh pengguna';
    }
    
    // Tampilkan hasil
    tampilkanHasilSyncTabel(results);
    
    return results;
    
  } catch (error) {
    const errorMsg = `❌ Sync tabel baru gagal: ${error.toString()}`;
    console.error(errorMsg);
    
    SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().toast(
      'Sync tabel baru gagal! Lihat log untuk detail.',
      'Error',
      5
    );
    
    return { success: false, error: errorMsg };
  }
}

function syncTabelTerdefinisi() {
  try {
    console.log('🔄 Memulai sync tabel terdefinisi...');
    const spreadsheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    
    // Daftar tabel yang sudah dikonfirmasi dan memiliki endpoint valid
    const tabelBaru = [
      { 
        tableName: 'jadwal_madin',
        sheetName: 'Data_Jadwal_Madin',
        endpoint: 'get_jadwal_madin',
        color: '#3F51B5'
      },
      { 
        tableName: 'jadwal_quran',
        sheetName: 'Data_Jadwal_Quran',
        endpoint: 'get_jadwal_quran',
        color: '#9C27B0'
      },
      { 
        tableName: 'jadwal_kegiatan',
        sheetName: 'Data_Jadwal_Kegiatan',
        endpoint: 'get_jadwal_kegiatan',
        color: '#FF9800'
      },
      { 
        tableName: 'absensi_guru',
        sheetName: 'Data_Absensi_Guru',
        endpoint: 'get_absensi_guru',
        color: '#795548'
      },
      { 
        tableName: 'pengaturan_absensi_otomatis',
        sheetName: 'Data_Pengaturan_Absensi_Otomatis',
        endpoint: 'get_pengaturan_absensi_otomatis',
        color: '#607D8B'
      },
      { 
        tableName: 'login_attempts',
        sheetName: 'Data_Login_Attempts',
        endpoint: 'get_login_attempts',
        color: '#F44336'
      },
      { 
        tableName: 'pengaturan_notifikasi',
        sheetName: 'Data_Pengaturan_Notifikasi',
        endpoint: 'get_pengaturan_notifikasi',
        color: '#2196F3'
      }
    ];
    
    const results = [];
    
    for (const tabel of tabelBaru) {
      try {
        console.log(`📋 Memproses ${tabel.tableName}...`);
        
        // Cek apakah sheet sudah ada
        const existingSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName(tabel.sheetName);
        if (existingSheet) {
          console.log(`⏭️ ${tabel.sheetName} sudah ada, skip`);
          results.push({
            table: tabel.tableName,
            status: 'SKIPPED',
            message: 'Sheet sudah ada',
            dataCount: 0
          });
          continue;
        }
        
        // Test endpoint terlebih dahulu
        const testResult = testSpecificEndpoint(tabel.endpoint);
        if (!testResult.success) {
          console.log(`⚠️ Endpoint ${tabel.endpoint} tidak tersedia`);
          results.push({
            table: tabel.tableName,
            status: 'FAILED',
            message: `Endpoint tidak tersedia: ${testResult.error}`,
            dataCount: 0
          });
          continue;
        }
        
        // Ambil data dari API
        const url = `${API_BASE_URL}?action=${tabel.endpoint}&limit=5000`;
        const options = {
          'muteHttpExceptions': true,
          'timeout': 30000
        };
        
        const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
        const result = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
        
        if (result.success && result.data) {
          const data = result.data || [];
          
          if (data.length === 0) {
            // Buat sheet kosong dengan struktur yang benar
            const sheet = spreadsheet.insertSheet(tabel.sheetName);
            
            // Coba dapatkan struktur tabel dari database
            const structure = getDatabaseTableStructure(tabel.tableName);
            let headers = [];
            
            if (structure && structure.length > 0) {
              headers = structure.map(col => col.Field || col.column_name);
            } else {
              // Fallback: ambil headers dari data pertama atau gunakan default
              if (data.length > 0) {
                headers = Object.keys(data[0]);
              } else {
                // Gunakan header umum
                headers = ['id', 'nama', 'created_at', 'updated_at'];
              }
            }
            
            // Set headers
            sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length)
              .setValues([headers])
              .setFontWeight('bold')
              .setBackground(tabel.color)
              .setFontColor('white');
            
            // Auto resize
            for (let col = 1; col <= headers.length; col++) {
              sheet.autoResizeColumn(col);
            }
            
            results.push({
              table: tabel.tableName,
              status: 'CREATED_EMPTY',
              message: 'Sheet dibuat (kosong)',
              dataCount: 0
            });
          } else {
            // Buat sheet dengan data
            const sheet = spreadsheet.insertSheet(tabel.sheetName);
            
            const headers = Object.keys(data[0]);
            
            // Set headers
            sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length)
              .setValues([headers])
              .setFontWeight('bold')
              .setBackground(tabel.color)
              .setFontColor('white');
            
            // Fill data
            const rows = data.map(row => 
              headers.map(header => {
                let value = row[header] || '';
                
                if (isLongNumericField(header, value)) {
                  value = formatForSheetDisplay(value);
                }
                
                return value;
              })
            );
            
            if (rows.length > 0) {
              sheet.getRange(2, 1, rows.length, headers.length).setValues(rows);
            }
            
            // Set column formats
            setColumnFormats(sheet, headers);
            
            // Auto resize
            for (let col = 1; col <= headers.length; col++) {
              sheet.autoResizeColumn(col);
            }
            
            results.push({
              table: tabel.tableName,
              status: 'SUCCESS',
              message: 'Data berhasil disinkronisasi',
              dataCount: data.length
            });
          }
        } else {
          results.push({
            table: tabel.tableName,
            status: 'FAILED',
            message: result.error || 'Unknown error',
            dataCount: 0
          });
        }
        
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(`❌ Error memproses ${tabel.tableName}: ${error.toString()}`);
        results.push({
          table: tabel.tableName || 'Unknown',
          status: 'ERROR',
          message: error.toString().substring(0, 100),
          dataCount: 0
        });
      }
      
      Utilities.sleep(1500); // Delay antar request
    }
    
    return {
      success: true,
      method: 'DEFINED_TABLES',
      results: results,
      summary: {
        total: results.length,
        success: results.filter(r => r.status === 'SUCCESS' || r.status === 'CREATED_EMPTY').length,
        failed: results.filter(r => r.status === 'FAILED' || r.status === 'ERROR').length,
        skipped: results.filter(r => r.status === 'SKIPPED').length
      }
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(`❌ Error sync tabel terdefinisi: ${error.toString()}`);
    return { success: false, error: error.toString() };
  }
}

function syncTabelOtomatis() {
  try {
    console.log('🔍 Memulai sync tabel otomatis...');
    const spreadsheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    
    // Dapatkan daftar tabel dari database
    const tables = getAvailableTables();
    
    if (!tables || tables.length === 0) {
      return {
        success: false,
        message: 'Tidak dapat mengambil daftar tabel dari database'
      };
    }
    
    console.log(`📊 Ditemukan ${tables.length} tabel di database`);
    
    // Filter tabel yang belum ada di spreadsheet
    const existingSheets = spreadsheet.getSheets().map(s => s.getName());
    const tablesToSync = tables.filter(table => {
      const expectedSheetName = `Data_${capitalizeFirstLetter(table)}`;
      return !existingSheets.includes(expectedSheetName);
    });
    
    console.log(`🔄 ${tablesToSync.length} tabel baru akan disinkronisasi`);
    
    const results = [];
    
    for (const tableName of tablesToSync) {
      try {
        const sheetName = `Data_${capitalizeFirstLetter(tableName)}`;
        console.log(`📋 Memproses ${tableName} -> ${sheetName}...`);
        
        // Coba endpoint standar
        const endpoint = `get_${tableName}`;
        const testResult = testSpecificEndpoint(endpoint);
        
        if (!testResult.success) {
          console.log(`⚠️ Endpoint ${endpoint} tidak tersedia untuk ${tableName}`);
          results.push({
            table: tableName,
            status: 'SKIPPED',
            message: 'Endpoint tidak tersedia',
            dataCount: 0
          });
          continue;
        }
        
        // Ambil data
        const url = `${API_BASE_URL}?action=${endpoint}&limit=1000`;
        const options = {
          'muteHttpExceptions': true,
          'timeout': 30000
        };
        
        const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(url, options);
        const result = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
        
        if (result.success && result.data) {
          const data = result.data || [];
          const sheet = spreadsheet.insertSheet(sheetName);
          
          if (data.length > 0) {
            const headers = Object.keys(data[0]);
            
            // Set headers
            sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length)
              .setValues([headers])
              .setFontWeight('bold')
              .setBackground('#4CAF50')
              .setFontColor('white');
            
            // Fill data
            const rows = data.map(row => 
              headers.map(header => row[header] || '')
            );
            
            if (rows.length > 0) {
              sheet.getRange(2, 1, rows.length, headers.length).setValues(rows);
            }
            
            // Auto resize
            for (let col = 1; col <= headers.length; col++) {
              sheet.autoResizeColumn(col);
            }
            
            results.push({
              table: tableName,
              status: 'SUCCESS',
              message: 'Data berhasil disinkronisasi',
              dataCount: data.length
            });
          } else {
            // Buat sheet kosong dengan struktur dari database
            const structure = getDatabaseTableStructure(tableName);
            let headers = [];
            
            if (structure && structure.length > 0) {
              headers = structure.map(col => col.Field || col.column_name);
            } else {
              headers = ['id', 'created_at', 'updated_at'];
            }
            
            sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length)
              .setValues([headers])
              .setFontWeight('bold')
              .setBackground('#9E9E9E')
              .setFontColor('white');
            
            // Auto resize
            for (let col = 1; col <= headers.length; col++) {
              sheet.autoResizeColumn(col);
            }
            
            results.push({
              table: tableName,
              status: 'CREATED_EMPTY',
              message: 'Sheet dibuat (kosong)',
              dataCount: 0
            });
          }
        }
        
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(`❌ Error sync ${tableName}: ${error.toString()}`);
        results.push({
          table: tableName,
          status: 'ERROR',
          message: error.toString().substring(0, 100),
          dataCount: 0
        });
      }
      
      Utilities.sleep(2000);
    }
    
    return {
      success: true,
      method: 'AUTOMATIC',
      results: results,
      summary: {
        total: tablesToSync.length,
        success: results.filter(r => r.status === 'SUCCESS' || r.status === 'CREATED_EMPTY').length,
        failed: results.filter(r => r.status === 'FAILED' || r.status === 'ERROR').length,
        skipped: results.filter(r => r.status === 'SKIPPED').length
      }
    };
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(`❌ Error sync tabel otomatis: ${error.toString()}`);
    return { success: false, error: error.toString() };
  }
}

// Fungsi bantuan baru
function getAvailableTables() {
  try {
    // Coba ambil daftar tabel dari API
    const payload = {
      action: 'get_tables_list'
    };
    
    const options = {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      payload: JSON.stringify(payload),
      'muteHttpExceptions': true,
      'timeout': 15000
    };
    
    const response = UrlFetchApp.fetch(API_BASE_URL, options);
    const result = JSON.parse(response.getContentText());
    
    if (result.success && result.tables) {
      return result.tables;
    }
    
    // Fallback: return tabel-tabel yang umum di PPMA
    return [
      'jadwal_madin', 'jadwal_quran', 'jadwal_kegiatan',
      'absensi_guru', 'pengaturan_absensi_otomatis',
      'login_attempts', 'pengaturan_notifikasi'
    ];
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.log(`⚠️ Tidak bisa dapatkan daftar tabel: ${error.toString()}`);
    return null;
  }
}

function capitalizeFirstLetter(string) {
  return string.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + string.slice(1);
}

function tampilkanHasilSyncTabel(results) {
  try {
    const sheet = buatSummarySheet();
    sheet.clear();
    
    let row = 1;
    sheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue('📊 HASIL SINKRONISASI TABEL BARU').setFontWeight("bold").setFontSize(16);
    row += 2;
    
    sheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue(`Metode: ${results.method || 'Unknown'}`);
    row++;
    sheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue(`Waktu: ${new Date().toLocaleString()}`);
    row += 2;
    
    // Summary
    if (results.summary) {
      sheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue('📈 SUMMARY:').setFontWeight("bold");
      row++;
      sheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue(`Total: ${results.summary.total}`);
      row++;
      sheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue(`Berhasil: ${results.summary.success} ✅`);
      row++;
      sheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue(`Gagal: ${results.summary.failed} ❌`);
      row++;
      sheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue(`Dilewati: ${results.summary.skipped} ⏭️`);
      row += 2;
    }
    
    // Detail
    sheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue('📋 DETAIL PER TABEL:').setFontWeight("bold");
    row++;
    
    if (results.results && results.results.length > 0) {
      results.results.forEach(result => {
        let statusIcon = '❓';
        let statusColor = '#000000';
        
        switch (result.status) {
          case 'SUCCESS':
            statusIcon = '✅';
            statusColor = '#4CAF50';
            break;
          case 'CREATED_EMPTY':
            statusIcon = '📝';
            statusColor = '#FF9800';
            break;
          case 'SKIPPED':
            statusIcon = '⏭️';
            statusColor = '#9E9E9E';
            break;
          case 'FAILED':
          case 'ERROR':
            statusIcon = '❌';
            statusColor = '#F44336';
            break;
        }
        
        const cell = sheet.getRange(row, 1);
        cell.setValue(`${statusIcon} ${result.table}: ${result.message} (${result.dataCount} data)`);
        cell.setFontColor(statusColor);
        row++;
      });
    }
    
    sheet.autoResizeColumn(1);
    
    // Toast notification
    const successCount = results.results?.filter(r => 
      r.status === 'SUCCESS' || r.status === 'CREATED_EMPTY'
    ).length || 0;
    
    SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().toast(
      `Sync tabel selesai: ${successCount} tabel berhasil`,
      '✅ Sync Tabel Baru',
      5
    );
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(`❌ Error tampilkan hasil: ${error.toString()}`);
  }
}

function syncSingleTableFinal(sheetName) {
  // Implementasi sederhana untuk sync single table
  try {
    const tableMap = {
      'Data_Guru': 'guru',
      'Data_Murid': 'murid', 
      'Data_Users': 'users',
      'Data_Alumni': 'alumni'
    };
    
    const tableName = tableMap[sheetName];
    if (!tableName) {
      return `ERROR: Tidak ada mapping untuk ${sheetName}`;
    }
    
    return syncDataUmumViaAPI(`get_${tableName}`, sheetName, '#4CAF50');
  } catch (error) {
    return `ERROR: ${error.toString()}`;
  }
}

function showSettingsDialog() {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();

      <h2>⚙️ Pengaturan Sistem PPMA</h2>
      <p>Fitur pengaturan akan segera tersedia.</p>
      <button onclick="google.script.host.close()" style="padding: 10px 20px; background: #4CAF50; color: white; border: none; border-radius: 4px;">
        Tutup
      </button>
    </div>
  `)
  .setWidth(400)
  .setHeight(200);
  
  ui.showModalDialog(html, 'Pengaturan Sistem');
}

function createAlumniTransferReport(result, statusKeluar, keterangan, tahunKeluar) {
  try {
    const spreadsheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const timestamp = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyyMMdd_HHmmss');
    const reportSheetName = `LAPORAN_ALUMNI_${timestamp}`;
    
    // Cek apakah sheet laporan sudah ada
    let reportSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName(reportSheetName);
    if (!reportSheet) {
      reportSheet = spreadsheet.insertSheet(reportSheetName);
    }
    
    // Clear sheet
    reportSheet.clear();
    
    // Header
    let row = 1;
    reportSheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue('📊 LAPORAN PEMINDAHAN KE ALUMNI').setFontWeight("bold").setFontSize(14);
    row += 2;
    
    // Informasi umum
    reportSheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue('Tanggal Proses:').setFontWeight("bold");
    reportSheet.getRange(row, 2).setValue(new Date().toLocaleString());
    row++;
    
    reportSheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue('Status Keluar:').setFontWeight("bold");
    reportSheet.getRange(row, 2).setValue(statusKeluar);
    row++;
    
    reportSheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue('Tahun Keluar:').setFontWeight("bold");
    reportSheet.getRange(row, 2).setValue(tahunKeluar);
    row++;
    
    reportSheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue('Keterangan:').setFontWeight("bold");
    reportSheet.getRange(row, 2).setValue(keterangan || '(tidak ada)');
    row += 2;
    
    // Ringkasan
    reportSheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue('📈 RINGKASAN').setFontWeight("bold");
    row++;
    
    reportSheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue('Total Diproses:');
    reportSheet.getRange(row, 2).setValue(result.totalProcessed);
    row++;
    
    reportSheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue('Berhasil:');
    reportSheet.getRange(row, 2).setValue(result.successCount).setFontColor('#4CAF50');
    row++;
    
    reportSheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue('Gagal:');
    reportSheet.getRange(row, 2).setValue(result.errorCount).setFontColor('#F44336');
    row += 2;
    
    // Detail murid yang berhasil
    if (result.processedMurids && result.processedMurids.length > 0) {
      reportSheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue('✅ MURID YANG BERHASIL DIPINDAHKAN').setFontWeight("bold");
      row++;
      
      // Header tabel
      reportSheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue('No').setFontWeight("bold");
      reportSheet.getRange(row, 2).setValue('ID Murid').setFontWeight("bold");
      reportSheet.getRange(row, 3).setValue('Nama').setFontWeight("bold");
      reportSheet.getRange(row, 4).setValue('NIS').setFontWeight("bold");
      reportSheet.getRange(row, 5).setValue('Status').setFontWeight("bold");
      row++;
      
      // Isi data
      result.processedMurids.forEach((murid, index) => {
        reportSheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue(index + 1);
        reportSheet.getRange(row, 2).setValue(murid.id);
        reportSheet.getRange(row, 3).setValue(murid.nama);
        
        // Cari NIS dari sheet Data_Murid
        const muridSheet = spreadsheet.getSheetByName('Data_Murid');
        if (muridSheet) {
          const data = muridSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
          const headers = data[0];
          const nisIndex = headers.indexOf('nis');
          const idIndex = headers.indexOf('murid_id');
          
          for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
            if (data[i][idIndex] == murid.id && nisIndex !== -1) {
              reportSheet.getRange(row, 4).setValue(data[i][nisIndex]);
              break;
            }
          }
        }
        
        reportSheet.getRange(row, 5).setValue('✅ Berhasil').setFontColor('#4CAF50');
        row++;
      });
    }
    
    // Format kolom
    for (let col = 1; col <= 5; col++) {
      reportSheet.autoResizeColumn(col);
    }
    
    // Beri warna header
    reportSheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5).setBackground('#4CAF50').setFontColor('white');
    
    console.log(`✅ Laporan alumni disimpan di sheet: ${reportSheetName}`);
    
    // Tampilkan toast notifikasi
    SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().toast(
      `✅ ${result.successCount} murid berhasil dipindahkan ke alumni`,
      'Pindah ke Alumni',
      8
    );
    
    return reportSheetName;
    
  } catch (error) {
    console.error(`❌ Error membuat laporan: ${error.toString()}`);
    return null;
  }
}

function showTestAlumniAPIResult() {
  try {
    console.log('🧪 Menjalankan test API Alumni...');
    
    // Jalankan test
    const result = testAlumniAPI();
    
    // Buat summary
    let summary = '🧪 HASIL TESTING API ALUMNI\n\n';
    summary += `GET Alumni: ${result.getAlumni.success ? '✅' : '❌'} (HTTP ${result.getAlumni.code})\n`;
    summary += `📊 Data ditemukan: ${result.getAlumni.dataCount}\n\n`;
    summary += `INSERT Alumni: ${result.insertAlumni.success ? '✅' : '❌'} (HTTP ${result.insertAlumni.code})\n\n`;
    summary += `DELETE Murid: ${result.deleteMurid.success ? '✅' : '❌'} (HTTP ${result.deleteMurid.code})\n\n`;
    
    if (result.error) {
      summary += `❌ Error: ${result.error}\n`;
    }
    
    summary += `\n🕐 Waktu test: ${new Date().toLocaleString()}`;
    
    // Tampilkan di sheet SUMMARY
    const sheet = buatSummarySheet();
    sheet.clear();
    
    let row = 1;
    sheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue('🧪 HASIL TESTING API ALUMNI').setFontWeight("bold").setFontSize(16);
    row += 2;
    
    const lines = summary.split('\n');
    lines.forEach(line => {
      if (line.includes('✅')) {
        sheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue(line).setFontColor('#4CAF50');
      } else if (line.includes('❌')) {
        sheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue(line).setFontColor('#F44336');
      } else {
        sheet.getRange(row, 1).setValue(line);
      }
      row++;
    });
    
    sheet.autoResizeColumn(1);
    
    // Tampilkan toast
    SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().toast(
      'Testing API Alumni selesai. Lihat sheet SUMMARY.',
      '✅ Test Selesai',
      5
    );
    
    return summary;
    
  } catch (error) {
    const errorMsg = `❌ Error showTestAlumniAPIResult: ${error.toString()}`;
    console.error(errorMsg);
    
    SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().toast(
      'Error testing API Alumni',
      '❌ Test Gagal',
      5
    );
    
    return errorMsg;
  }
}
